<h1 style='mso-list:l26 level1 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022780"><![if !supportLists]><span

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022781"><![if !supportLists]><span

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>关闭顶部通知条</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>点击顶部通知条中的“</span><span lang=EN-US>X </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>不再提醒”后，刷新页面不再出现此通知条（使用本地</span><span
lang=EN-US>cookie</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>效果见视觉稿</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022782"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

lang=EN-US>/</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc433022782'><span

Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>登录</span></span></h2>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:63.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-list:l18 level3 lfo46'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>u<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>点击关注按钮：首先判断登录的</span><span
lang=EN-US>cookie</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>是否已设置（</span><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US>loginSuc</span></span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>）</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:63.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-list:l18 level3 lfo46'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>u<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>如果未设置登录</span><span lang=EN-US>cookie</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，则弹出登录框，使用给定的用户名和密码（需要表单验证）调用服务器</span><span
lang=EN-US>Ajax</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>登录，成功后设置登录</span><span
lang=EN-US>cookie</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:63.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-list:l18 level3 lfo46'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>登录成功后，调用关注</span><span lang=EN-US>API</span><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，并设置关注成功的</span><span lang=EN-US>cookie</span><span

mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>（</span><span class=SpellE><span
lang=EN-US>followSuc</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>）</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:63.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-list:l18 level3 lfo46'><![if !supportLists]><span

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022783"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>顶部右侧导航及内容区各产品的“了解更多”</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;

lang=EN-US>MOOC</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

lang=EN-US>hover</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>效果见视觉稿。点击“了解更多</span><span
lang=EN-US>&gt;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>”的跳转链接及打开方式相同。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>网易公开课：</span><span lang=EN-US><a
href="http://open.163.com/">http://open.163.com/</a></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>网易云课堂：</span><span lang=EN-US><a

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span

Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>中国大学</span><span lang=EN-US>MOOC</span><span

mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>：</span><span lang=EN-US><a
href="http://www.icourse163.org/">http://www.icourse163.org/</a></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022784"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.4<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>轮播图</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>三张轮播图轮播效果：实现每</span><span lang=EN-US>5s</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>切换图片，图片循环播放；鼠标悬停某张图片，则暂停切换；切换效果使用入场图片</span><span
lang=EN-US>500ms</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>淡入的方式。点击后新开窗口打开目的页面，对应的跳转链接如下，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US>banner1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US>banner2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US>banner3</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022785"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.5<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>左侧内容区</span><span
lang=EN-US>tab</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc433022785'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>切换</span></span></h2>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>点击“产品设计”或“编程语言”</span><span
lang=EN-US>tab</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，实现下方课程内容的更换。</span><span
lang=EN-US>tab</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>项的</span><span
lang=EN-US>hover</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>及选中效果见视觉稿，</span><span
lang=EN-US>tab</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>项对应的课程卡片数据见本文档的数据接口列表</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022786"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.6<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>查看课程详情</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>鼠标悬停“产品设计”或“编程语言”</span><span
lang=EN-US>tab</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>下的任意课程卡片，出现浮层显示该课程的课程详情；鼠标离开课程详情浮层，则浮层关闭。课程卡片即详情浮层的效果见视觉稿，课程卡片及详情数据见本文档的数据接口列表</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022787"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.7<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>右侧“机构介绍”中的视频介绍</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>点击“机构介绍”中的整块图片区域，调用浮层播放介绍视频。图片的</span><span
lang=EN-US>hover</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>效果见视觉稿，浮层中调用的播放器（不做浏览器兼容</span><span
lang=EN-US>,</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>可用</span><span
lang=EN-US>html5</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>）及视频内容接口见本文档的数据接口列表</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022788"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.8<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>右侧“热门推荐”</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:21.0pt'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>实现每次进入或刷新本页面，“热门推荐”模块中，接口返回</span><span
lang=EN-US>20</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>门课程数据，默认展示前</span><span
lang=EN-US>10</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:

lang=EN-US>5</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>秒更新一门课程，实现滚动更新热门课程的效果。课程数据接口见本文档的数据接口列表</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022789"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.9<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>页面布局动态适应</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:0'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>根据浏览器窗口宽度，适应两种视觉布局尺寸。窗口宽度</span><span
lang=EN-US>&lt;1205</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>时，使用小屏视觉布局；窗口宽度</span><span
lang=EN-US>&gt;=1205</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>时，使用大屏视觉布局。布局示意图见视觉效果</span></p>

<h1 style='mso-list:l26 level1 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022790"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<h1 style='mso-list:l26 level1 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022796"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;

style='mso-list:Ignore'>3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>大作业要求</span></a></h1>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022797"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.1<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>效果要求</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>正确还原视觉效果，正确测量大小宽高距离位置等数值，文字边框背景等颜色能正确取色。</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022798"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.2<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>功能要求</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>按照效果图和上面的功能点完成所有功能（可以不考虑跨域问题）。</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022799"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.3<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>兼容性要求</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>页面兼容</span><span
lang=EN-US>IE8+</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>、</span><span
lang=EN-US>FF</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>、</span><span
lang=EN-US>Chrome</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>，允许圆角、阴影只在高版本浏览器中实现。</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022800"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.4<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>HTML</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc433022800'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>要求</span></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>完善的头部信息，代码缩进，正确使用语义化标签及实体，考虑</span><span
lang=EN-US>SEO</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>需要，正确嵌套标签，正确使用标签属性，规范的注释格式。</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022801"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.5<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>CSS</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc433022801'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>要求</span></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>CSS</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>文件内部规范化分类，命名和格式规范化，注释清晰，合理优化代码。</span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:l26 level2 lfo24'><a name="_Toc433022802"><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-theme-font:major-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.6<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US>JS</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc433022802'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Cambria;mso-ascii-theme-font:major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
major-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-theme-font:major-latin'>要求</span></span></h2>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;
mso-char-indent-count:0;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo11'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>本作业要求不使用任何的</span><span
lang=EN-US>JS</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin'>框架</span></p>
